	<script>
	(function(){
		try{
			var url=location.pathname;
			var ua=navigator.userAgent;
			var sampleRate=0.1;
			var lcp;
			function send(type,value){
				var payload={type:type,value:value,url:url,ua:ua,ts:Date.now()};
				if(Math.random()<sampleRate && navigator.sendBeacon){
					var blob=new Blob([JSON.stringify(payload)],{type:'application/json'});
					//navigator.sendBeacon('/api/perf-metrics.php',blob);
				}
				// console.log('[perf]',type,Math.round(value));
			}
			new PerformanceObserver(function(list){
				list.getEntries().forEach(function(entry){
					if(entry.name==='first-contentful-paint'){send('FCP',entry.startTime);}
				});
			}).observe({type:'paint',buffered:true});
			var lpo=new PerformanceObserver(function(list){
				var entries=list.getEntries();
				var last=entries[entries.length-1];
				if(last){lcp=last.startTime;}
			});
			lpo.observe({type:'largest-contentful-paint',buffered:true});
			function finalize(){
				if(lcp!==undefined){send('LCP',lcp);}
				lpo.disconnect();
			}
			document.addEventListener('visibilitychange',function(){
				if(document.visibilityState==='hidden'){finalize();}
			});
			window.addEventListener('pagehide',finalize);
		}catch(e){}
	})();
	</script>

	function getlike(str, no) {
		
		if (str == "") {
			return;
			} else {
			if (window.XMLHttpRequest) {
				// code for IE7+, Firefox, Chrome, Opera, Safari
				xmlhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
				} else {
				// code for IE6, IE5
				xmlhttp = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
			}
			
			if (typeof fbq === 'function') {
				fbq('track', 'AddToCart');
			}
			xmlhttp.open("GET","getlike.php?auth=XSRY3Z7J2JFSMCJGPVKU&phonenumber="+str,true);
			xmlhttp.send();
		}
	}

<script>
$(function() {
  function getUrlParam(name){
    var qs = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    var v = qs.get(name);
    return v ? String(v) : '';
  }
  function normalizeLocale(raw){
    var v = (raw || '').toLowerCase();
    if (!v) return '';
    if (v === 'zh-hk' || v === 'zh-cn' || v === 'en-hk' || v === 'en-uk' || v === 'en-au' || v === 'en-sg' || v === 'zh-sg' || v === 'zh-my') return v;
    if (v.indexOf('zh-hant') === 0) return 'zh-hk';
    if (v.indexOf('zh-hans') === 0) {
      if (v.indexOf('-sg') > -1) return 'zh-sg';
      if (v.indexOf('-my') > -1) return 'zh-my';
      return 'zh-cn';
    }
    if (v.indexOf('en-gb') === 0) return 'en-uk';
    if (v.indexOf('en-au') === 0) return 'en-au';
    if (v.indexOf('en-sg') === 0) return 'en-sg';
    if (v.indexOf('en-hk') === 0) return 'en-hk';
    return '';
  }
  function pathSegments(){
    try {
      var segs = (window.location.pathname || '').split('/');
      var out = [];
      for(var i=0;i<segs.length;i++){ if(segs[i]) out.push(segs[i]); }
      return out;
    } catch(e){ return []; }
  }
  function currentLocale() {
    var fromUrl = normalizeLocale(getUrlParam('locale'));
    if (fromUrl) return fromUrl;
    var segs = pathSegments();
    var locFromPath = normalizeLocale(segs[0] || '');
    if (locFromPath) return locFromPath;
    var m = document.querySelector('meta[http-equiv="content-language"]');
    var meta = m ? (m.getAttribute('content') || 'zh-hk') : 'zh-hk';
    var norm = normalizeLocale(meta);
    return norm || 'zh-hk';
  }
  function localeToArea(locale){
    switch(locale){
      case 'zh-hk':
      case 'en-hk':
        return '852';
      case 'zh-cn': return '86';
      case 'zh-my': return '60';
      case 'zh-sg':
      case 'en-sg': return '65';
      case 'en-au': return '61';
      case 'en-uk': return '44';
      default: return '';
    }
  }
  function slugToAreaCode(slug){
    switch(String(slug || '')){
      case 'hong-kong': return '852';
      case 'mainland-china': return '86';
      case 'macau': return '853';
      case 'malaysia': return '60';
      case 'singapore': return '65';
      case 'thailand': return '66';
      case 'united-kingdom': return '44';
      case 'australia': return '61';
      default: return '';
    }
  }
  function currentAreaCode(){
    var ac = getUrlParam('areacode').replace(/[^0-9]/g,'');
    if (ac) return ac;
    var segs = pathSegments();
    var slug = segs[1] || '';
    var bySlug = slugToAreaCode(slug);
    if (bySlug) return bySlug;
    var loc = currentLocale();
    var mapped = localeToArea(loc);
    if (mapped) return mapped;
    var cookie = (typeof getCookieAreaCode === 'function') ? (getCookieAreaCode() || '') : '';
    cookie = (cookie || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g,'');
    return cookie || '852';
  }
  function areaCodeToSlug(code){
    switch(String(code)){
      case '852': return 'hong-kong';
      case '86': return 'mainland-china';
      case '853': return 'macau';
      case '60': return 'malaysia';
      case '65': return 'singapore';
      case '66': return 'thailand';
      case '44': return 'united-kingdom';
      case '61': return 'australia';
      default: return 'hong-kong';
    }
  }
  function areaCodeToScript(code){
    switch(String(code)){
      case '852': return 'pricebook-hongkong';
      case '86': return 'pricebook-mainland-china';
      case '853': return 'pricebook-macau';
      case '60': return 'pricebook-malaysia';
      case '65': return 'pricebook-singapore';
      case '66': return 'pricebook-thailand';
      case '44': return 'pricebook-uk';
      case '61': return 'pricebook-australia';
      default: return 'pricebook-hongkong';
    }
  }
  // UNUSED: baseUrl param not used
  function navigateWith(locale, code, baseUrl) {
    try { setCookieAreaCode(code); } catch(e) {}
    var q = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    q.delete('locale');
    q.delete('areacode');
    var region = areaCodeToSlug(code);
    var script = areaCodeToScript(code);
    var url = '/' + String(locale) + '/' + region + '/lucky-phone-number/' + script;
    var qs = q.toString();
    window.location.href = qs ? (url + '?' + qs) : url;
  }
  function markSelected(container) {
    var selCode = currentAreaCode();
    var selLocale = currentLocale();
    var any = false;
    container.querySelectorAll('.lang-link').forEach(function(a){
      var match = (a.dataset.code === selCode && a.dataset.locale === selLocale);
      a.setAttribute('aria-selected', match ? 'true' : 'false');
      if(match) any = true;
    });
    if(!any){
      var fallback = container.querySelector('.lang-link[data-code="852"][data-locale="zh-hk"]');
      if(fallback){ fallback.setAttribute('aria-selected','true'); }
    }
  }
  function setupDropdown(rootId) {
    var root = document.getElementById(rootId);
    if(!root) return;
    var btn = root.querySelector('.area-dropdown-btn');
    var panel = root.querySelector('.area-dropdown-content');
    btn.setAttribute('aria-haspopup','listbox');
    btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
    btn.setAttribute('aria-controls', panel.id);
    btn.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      e.preventDefault();
      var open = root.classList.toggle('open');
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', open ? 'true':'false');
      if(open) {
        var first = panel.querySelector('.lang-link'); if(first) first.focus();
      }
    });
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      if(!root.contains(e.target)) { root.classList.remove('open'); btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false'); }
    });
    panel.addEventListener('keydown', function(e){
      var items = Array.prototype.slice.call(panel.querySelectorAll('.lang-link'));
      var idx = items.indexOf(document.activeElement);
      if(e.key === 'ArrowRight' || e.key === 'ArrowDown') { e.preventDefault(); var next = items[idx+1] || items[0]; next.focus(); }
      if(e.key === 'ArrowLeft' || e.key === 'ArrowUp') { e.preventDefault(); var prev = items[idx-1] || items[items.length-1]; prev.focus(); }
      if(e.key === 'Escape') { root.classList.remove('open'); btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false'); btn.focus(); }
      if(e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
        var row = document.activeElement.closest('.area-row');
        if(row){
          e.preventDefault();
          var code = row.dataset.code;
          var url = row.dataset.url;
          var locale = (code==='86' || code==='60' || code==='65') ? 'zh-cn' : 'zh-hk';
          panel.querySelectorAll('.lang-link').forEach(function(a){ a.setAttribute('aria-selected','false'); });
          panel.querySelectorAll('.area-row').forEach(function(r){ r.setAttribute('aria-selected','false'); });
          row.setAttribute('aria-selected','true');
          root.classList.remove('open');
          btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
          setTimeout(function(){ navigateWith(locale, code, url); }, 10);
        }
      }
    });
    panel.querySelectorAll('.lang-link').forEach(function(el){
      el.addEventListener('click', function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        panel.querySelectorAll('.lang-link').forEach(function(a){ a.setAttribute('aria-selected','false'); });
        el.setAttribute('aria-selected','true');
        root.classList.remove('open');
        btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
        setTimeout(function(){ navigateWith(el.dataset.locale, el.dataset.code, el.dataset.url); }, 10);
      });
      el.addEventListener('keydown', function(e){
        if(e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
          e.preventDefault();
          panel.querySelectorAll('.lang-link').forEach(function(a){ a.setAttribute('aria-selected','false'); });
          el.setAttribute('aria-selected','true');
          root.classList.remove('open');
          btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
          setTimeout(function(){ navigateWith(el.dataset.locale, el.dataset.code, el.dataset.url); }, 10);
        }
      });
    });
    panel.addEventListener('click', function(e){
      var target = e.target;
      var row = target.closest('.area-row');
      if(row && (target.classList.contains('fi') || target.classList.contains('area-name') || target.classList.contains('code'))){
        e.preventDefault();
        var code = row.dataset.code;
        var url = row.dataset.url;
        var locale = (code==='86' || code==='60' || code==='65') ? 'zh-cn' : 'zh-hk';
        panel.querySelectorAll('.lang-link').forEach(function(a){ a.setAttribute('aria-selected','false'); });
        panel.querySelectorAll('.area-row').forEach(function(r){ r.setAttribute('aria-selected','false'); });
        row.setAttribute('aria-selected','true');
        root.classList.remove('open');
        btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
        setTimeout(function(){ navigateWith(locale, code, url); }, 10);
      }
    });
    markSelected(panel);
  }
  setupDropdown('areaDropdownDesktop');
  setupDropdown('areaDropdownMobile');
});
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const carousel = document.querySelector('#brand-carousel');
    if (!carousel) return;

    const container = carousel.querySelector('.brand-carousel__container');
    const trackContainer = carousel.querySelector('.brand-carousel__track-container');
    const track = carousel.querySelector('.brand-carousel__track');
    let slides = Array.from(track.children);
    const navLeft = carousel.querySelector('.brand-carousel__zone--middle-left');
    const navRight = carousel.querySelector('.brand-carousel__zone--middle-right');
    const loadingIndicator = carousel.querySelector('.brand-carousel__loading-indicator');
    const dotsNav = carousel.querySelector('.brand-carousel__nav');
    let dots = Array.from(dotsNav.children);

    let currentIndex = 0;
    let autoPlayInterval;
    const AUTO_PLAY_DELAY = 5000;
    let startX = 0;
    let isTransitioning = false;
    let isHovering = false;
    let playingVideos = new Set();
    let ytPlayers = {}; // Store player instances
    let pendingPlayers = []; // Queue for players before API is ready
    let videoMeta = {};

    // --- YouTube API Integration ---
    const loadYouTubeAPI = () => {
        if (!window.YT) {
            const tag = document.createElement('script');
            tag.src = "https://www.youtube.com/iframe_api";
            const firstScriptTag = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
            firstScriptTag.parentNode.insertBefore(tag, firstScriptTag);
        }
    };

    window.onYouTubeIframeAPIReady = () => {
        processPendingPlayers();
    };

    const processPendingPlayers = () => {
        if (window.YT && window.YT.Player) {
            while (pendingPlayers.length > 0) {
                const { id, videoId } = pendingPlayers.shift();
                // If videoId is null, we assume we are enhancing an existing iframe
                initYouTubePlayer(id, videoId);
            }
        }
    };

    const initYouTubePlayer = (iframeId, videoId) => {
        // Ensure element exists
        if (!document.getElementById(iframeId)) return;

        const config = {
            events: {
                'onStateChange': onPlayerStateChange,
                'onError': function(e){
                    let id = null;
                    try {
                        if (e.target._iframeId) {
                            id = e.target._iframeId;
                        } else if (e.target.getIframe && typeof e.target.getIframe === 'function') {
                            id = e.target.getIframe().id;
                        }
                    } catch(ex) {}
                    if (!id) {
                        id = Object.keys(ytPlayers).find(key => ytPlayers[key] === e.target) || null;
                    }
                    if (id) {
                        const el = document.getElementById('fallback-' + id);
                        if (el) { el.style.display = 'block'; }
                        stopAutoPlay();
                    }
                }
            }
        };
        // Only add videoId if we are creating a new player from scratch (div), 
        // OR if we want to force load a video. 
        // If we are enhancing an existing iframe, we don't need videoId in config usually, 
        // unless we want to reload it. 
        // But initYouTubePlayer is called with videoId for dynamic slides.
        if (videoId) {
            config.videoId = videoId;
        }

        const player = new YT.Player(iframeId, config);
        
        // Attach ID to the player instance for reliable tracking
        player._iframeId = iframeId;
        ytPlayers[iframeId] = player;
        if (videoId) { videoMeta[iframeId] = videoId; }
    };

    const onPlayerStateChange = (event) => {
        let iframeId = null;
        try {
            // Priority 1: Check attached ID
            if (event.target._iframeId) {
                iframeId = event.target._iframeId;
            }
            // Priority 2: Try getting ID from getIframe()
            else if (event.target.getIframe && typeof event.target.getIframe === 'function') {
                iframeId = event.target.getIframe().id;
            }
        } catch(e) { }

        // Fallback: Find ID by matching player instance
        if (!iframeId) {
            iframeId = Object.keys(ytPlayers).find(key => ytPlayers[key] === event.target);
        }

        if (event.data === YT.PlayerState.PLAYING || event.data === YT.PlayerState.BUFFERING) {
            if (iframeId) playingVideos.add(iframeId);
            stopAutoPlay();
        } else if (event.data === YT.PlayerState.PAUSED || event.data === YT.PlayerState.ENDED || event.data === YT.PlayerState.CUED) {
            if (iframeId) playingVideos.delete(iframeId);
            startAutoPlay(); // Attempt to resume
        }
    };

    // --- Dynamic Content Loading ---

    const getAreaCode = () => {
        // Priority 1: PHP detection (Context strict)
        const phpCode = '852';
        if (phpCode && phpCode !== '852') return phpCode;

        if (typeof currentAreaCode === 'function') {
            return currentAreaCode();
        }
        return '852'; // Default fallback
    };

    const fetchCarouselData = async () => {
        const areacode = getAreaCode();
        

        setLoading(true);
        const startTime = performance.now();
        const itemsToFetch = 6; // Number of items to fetch
        const startId = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000); // Random start ID

        try {
            // New Batch API Call
            // areacode: int, id: int, count: int
            //const url = `/api/get-carousell-record.php?areacode=${areacode}&id=${startId}&count=${itemsToFetch}`;
            const url = `/api/get-carousell-record.php?areacode=${areacode}&count=${itemsToFetch}`;
            
            const response = await fetch(url);
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`Network response was not ok: ${response.status}`);
            
            const data = await response.json();
            const endTime = performance.now();

            if (data.status === 'error') {
                throw new Error(data.message);
            }

            if (Array.isArray(data) && data.length > 0) {
                return data;
            } else {
                 // API returned empty or invalid data
            }
        } catch (error) {
            // Error fetching carousel data
        } finally {
            setLoading(false);
        }
        return [];
    };

    const extractVideoID = (url) => {
        try {
            const u = new URL(url, window.location.origin);
            const host = (u.hostname || '').replace(/^www\./, '');
            if (host.includes('youtube.com')) {
                const p = u.pathname || '';
                if (p.startsWith('/shorts/')) {
                    const id = (p.split('/')[2] || '').split('?')[0];
                    return id || null;
                }
                const v = u.searchParams.get('v');
                if (v) return v;
                if (p.startsWith('/embed/')) return (p.split('/')[2] || '').split('?')[0] || null;
            } else if (host.includes('youtu.be')) {
                const id = (u.pathname.split('/')[1] || '').split('?')[0];
                return id || null;
            }
        } catch(e) {}
        const regExp = /(?:shorts\/|youtu\.be\/|v\/|u\/\w\/|embed\/|watch\?.*v=|&v=)([^#&?]{11})/;
        const match = url.match(regExp);
        return match ? match[1] : null;
    };

    const createSlideElement = (item, index) => {
        const li = document.createElement('li');
        li.className = `brand-carousel__slide ${index === 0 ? 'current-slide' : ''}`;
        li.dataset.index = index;
        li.setAttribute('aria-hidden', index === 0 ? 'false' : 'true');

        if (item.type === 'image') {
            const linkWrapper = document.createElement('a');
            linkWrapper.href = item.content.link || '#';
            linkWrapper.style.display = 'block';
            linkWrapper.style.width = '100%';
            linkWrapper.style.height = '100%';
            linkWrapper.style.textDecoration = 'none';
            if (item.content.link) {
                linkWrapper.target = '_self'; // Or _blank if external
            }

            const img = document.createElement('img');
            img.className = 'brand-carousel__image';
            img.src = item.content.url;
            img.alt = 'Carousel Image';
            img.loading = 'lazy';
            img.style.objectFit = 'contain';
            img.style.background = '#ffffff';
            
            linkWrapper.appendChild(img);
            li.appendChild(linkWrapper);
        } else if (item.type === 'video') {
            const videoId = extractVideoID(item.content.url);
            const iframeId = `brand-video-${index}`;
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            div.className = 'brand-carousel__video-container';
            
            // Note: We use src initially, but YT.Player will take over.
            // We must add enablejsapi=1 to the src for the API to work if we didn't init with new YT.Player immediately.
            // But since we are using YT.Player to init, it can handle it.
            // However, to avoid double-loading or issues, we just render the iframe with ID.
            
            div.innerHTML = `
                <iframe 
                    id="${iframeId}"
                    class="brand-carousel__video-iframe"
                    src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/${videoId}?enablejsapi=1&rel=0&playsinline=1&modestbranding=1&origin=https://impressivecontact.com" 
                    title="Carousel Video" 
                    frameborder="0" 
                    allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" 
                    allowfullscreen
                    referrerpolicy="strict-origin-when-cross-origin"
                ></iframe>
                <div id="fallback-${iframeId}" class="brand-carousel__error" style="display:none;">
                    <p>錯誤 153 影片播放器設定錯誤，請按此於 YouTube 觀看：<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=${videoId}" target="_blank" rel="noopener">觀看影片</a></p>
                </div>`;
            li.appendChild(div);
            
            videoMeta[iframeId] = videoId;
            const iframeEl = div.querySelector(`#${iframeId}`);
            if (iframeEl) {
                iframeEl.addEventListener('load', function(){
                    pendingPlayers.push({ id: iframeId, videoId: videoId });
                    processPendingPlayers();
                }, { once: true });
            } else {
                pendingPlayers.push({ id: iframeId, videoId: videoId });
            }
        } else if (item.type === 'pricebook') {
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            div.className = 'brand-carousel__pricebook';
            let listHtml1 = '';
            let listHtml2 = '';
            if (item.content.pricebooks && Array.isArray(item.content.pricebooks)) {
                item.content.pricebooks.forEach((pb, idx) => {
                    const p = String(pb.price || '').replace(/[^0-9.]/g,'');
                    const n = parseFloat(p || '0');
                    const priceText = n > 2000000 ? '請查詢' : `$${pb.price}`;
                    const row = `
                        <li class="brand-carousel__pricebook-item">
                            <a class="brand-carousel__pricebook-link" href="pricebook" target="_self" aria-label="search ${pb.phonenumber}">
                                <span class="brand-carousel__pricebook-number">${pb.phonenumber}</span>
                                <span class="brand-carousel__pricebook-price">${priceText}</span>
                            </a>
                        </li>`;
                    if (idx % 2 === 0) listHtml1 += row; else listHtml2 += row;
                });
            }
            div.innerHTML = `
                <h2 class="brand-carousel__pricebook-title">${item.content.description}</h2>
                <div class="brand-carousel__pricebook-grid">
                    <ul class="brand-carousel__pricebook-list">
                        ${listHtml1}
                    </ul>
                    <ul class="brand-carousel__pricebook-list">
                        ${listHtml2}
                    </ul>
                </div>
            `;
            li.appendChild(div);
        }
        return li;
    };

    const renderCarousel = (items) => {
        if (!items || items.length === 0) return;

        // Clear existing track
        track.innerHTML = '';
        dotsNav.innerHTML = '';

        items.forEach((item, index) => {
            // Create Slide
            const slide = createSlideElement(item, index);
            track.appendChild(slide);

            // Create Dot
            const btn = document.createElement('button');
            btn.className = `brand-carousel__indicator ${index === 0 ? 'current-slide' : ''}`;
            btn.setAttribute('aria-label', `Go to slide ${index + 1}`);
            btn.setAttribute('aria-selected', index === 0 ? 'true' : 'false');
            btn.dataset.slideTarget = index;
            dotsNav.appendChild(btn);
        });

        // Update state variables
        slides = Array.from(track.children);
        dots = Array.from(dotsNav.children);
        currentIndex = 0;
        updateSlidePosition();
        startAutoPlay();
    };

    const initDynamicCarousel = () => {
        const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
            entries.forEach(entry => {
                if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                    observer.disconnect(); // Load only once
                    fetchCarouselData().then(data => {
                        if (data && data.length > 0) {
                            stopAutoPlay(); // Stop existing autoplay if any
                            renderCarousel(data);
                        }
                    });
                }
            });
        }, { rootMargin: '100px' });

        observer.observe(carousel);
    };

    // --- Core Functions ---

    const setLoading = (loading) => {
        if (loading) {
            loadingIndicator.classList.add('visible');
            container.classList.add('is-loading');
        } else {
            loadingIndicator.classList.remove('visible');
            container.classList.remove('is-loading');
        }
    };

    const stopAllVideos = () => {
        // Pause via postMessage for standard iframes
        const iframes = track.querySelectorAll('iframe');
        iframes.forEach(iframe => {
            try {
                if (iframe && iframe.contentWindow) {
                    // Check if origin is YouTube to avoid cross-origin errors
                    const src = iframe.src || '';
                    if (src.indexOf('youtube.com') > -1 || src.indexOf('youtu.be') > -1) {
                        iframe.contentWindow.postMessage('{"event":"command","func":"pauseVideo","args":""}', '*');
                    }
                }
            } catch(e) { }
        });
        
        // Also use API to pause if available
        Object.values(ytPlayers).forEach(player => {
            if (player && typeof player.pauseVideo === 'function') {
                try {
                     // Check if player is ready
                     if (player.getPlayerState && typeof player.getPlayerState === 'function') {
                         player.pauseVideo();
                     }
                } catch (e) {
                    // Error pausing YT player
                }
            }
        });
    };

    const updateSlidePosition = () => {
        track.style.transform = `translateX(-${currentIndex * 100}%)`;
        
        // Pause any playing videos when slide changes
        Object.values(ytPlayers).forEach(player => {
            if (player && typeof player.pauseVideo === 'function') {
                try {
                     if (player.getPlayerState && typeof player.getPlayerState === 'function') {
                         player.pauseVideo();
                     }
                } catch (e) {
                     // Ignore errors from unready players
                }
            }
        });
    };

    const updateDots = (index) => {
        const currentDot = dotsNav.querySelector('.current-slide');
        if (currentDot) {
            currentDot.classList.remove('current-slide');
            currentDot.setAttribute('aria-selected', 'false');
        }
        if (dots[index]) {
            dots[index].classList.add('current-slide');
            dots[index].setAttribute('aria-selected', 'true');
        }
    };

    const updateSlidesAria = (index) => {
        slides.forEach((slide, i) => {
            if (i === index) {
                slide.classList.add('current-slide');
                slide.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
            } else {
                slide.classList.remove('current-slide');
                slide.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
            }
        });
    };

    const moveToSlide = (index) => {
        if (isTransitioning) return;
        isTransitioning = true;
        setLoading(true);

        // Pause any playing videos before moving
        stopAllVideos();

        if (index < 0) index = slides.length - 1;
        if (index >= slides.length) index = 0;

        currentIndex = index;
        updateSlidePosition();
        updateDots(currentIndex);
        updateSlidesAria(currentIndex);

        setTimeout(() => {
            setLoading(false);
            isTransitioning = false;
        }, 300);
    };

    // --- Auto Play ---
    
    const startAutoPlay = () => {
        stopAutoPlay(); // Clear existing
        
        // 1. Check tracked playing state
        if (playingVideos.size > 0) return;
        
        // 2. Failsafe: Check actual player states (in case events were missed)
        const isAnyVideoPlaying = Object.values(ytPlayers).some(player => {
            try {
                if (player && typeof player.getPlayerState === 'function') {
                    const state = player.getPlayerState();
                    return state === YT.PlayerState.PLAYING || state === YT.PlayerState.BUFFERING;
                }
            } catch(e) {}
            return false;
        });
        if (isAnyVideoPlaying) return;

        // 3. Check Hover/Focus states
        // Use tracked isHovering flag AND native :hover check for robustness
        const nativeHover = carousel.matches ? carousel.matches(':hover') : false;
        
        // Check if focus is inside carousel (e.g. user clicked iframe or controls)
        const hasFocus = document.activeElement && carousel.contains(document.activeElement);

        if (isHovering || nativeHover || hasFocus) return;

        autoPlayInterval = setInterval(() => {
            moveToSlide(currentIndex + 1);
        }, AUTO_PLAY_DELAY);
    };

    const stopAutoPlay = () => {
        if (autoPlayInterval) {
            clearInterval(autoPlayInterval);
        }
    };

    // --- Event Listeners ---

    // Zone Clicks
    const debounce = (func, wait) => {
        let timeout;
        return function(...args) {
            const context = this;
            clearTimeout(timeout);
            timeout = setTimeout(() => func.apply(context, args), wait);
        };
    };

    const handleNav = (direction) => {
        if (direction === 'prev') moveToSlide(currentIndex - 1);
        else moveToSlide(currentIndex + 1);
        stopAutoPlay();
        startAutoPlay();
    };

    const debouncedNav = debounce(handleNav, 100);

    if (navLeft) {
        navLeft.addEventListener('click', () => debouncedNav('prev'));
        navLeft.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
             if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                e.preventDefault();
                debouncedNav('prev');
             }
        });
    }

    if (navRight) {
        navRight.addEventListener('click', () => debouncedNav('next'));
        navRight.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
             if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                e.preventDefault();
                debouncedNav('next');
             }
        });
    }

    // Dots
    if (dotsNav) {
        dotsNav.addEventListener('click', e => {
            const targetDot = e.target.closest('button');
            if (!targetDot) return;

            const targetIndex = parseInt(targetDot.dataset.slideTarget);
            moveToSlide(targetIndex);
            stopAutoPlay();
            startAutoPlay();
        });
    }

    // Keyboard Navigation
    carousel.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
        if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft') {
            moveToSlide(currentIndex - 1);
            stopAutoPlay();
            startAutoPlay();
        } else if (e.key === 'ArrowRight') {
            moveToSlide(currentIndex + 1);
            stopAutoPlay();
            startAutoPlay();
        }
    });

    // Hover Pause
    carousel.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
        isHovering = true;
        stopAutoPlay();
    });
    carousel.addEventListener('mouseleave', (e) => {
        // Iframe Hover Detection Fix:
        // When moving mouse into a cross-origin iframe (like YouTube), mouseleave fires.
        // We check if the mouse coordinates are still within the carousel's bounding rect.
        // If so, we assume the user is hovering over the iframe, so we keep isHovering = true.
        const rect = carousel.getBoundingClientRect();
        if (e.clientX >= rect.left && e.clientX <= rect.right && 
            e.clientY >= rect.top && e.clientY <= rect.bottom) {
            return;
        }

        isHovering = false;
        startAutoPlay();
    });
    
    // Also handle focus for accessibility
    carousel.addEventListener('focusin', () => {
        isHovering = true;
        stopAutoPlay();
    });
    carousel.addEventListener('focusout', () => {
        // We use a small timeout to check where focus went, or just assume leave
        setTimeout(() => {
            if (!carousel.contains(document.activeElement)) {
                isHovering = false;
                startAutoPlay();
            }
        }, 50);
    });

    // Touch / Swipe Support
    if (container) {
        container.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
            startX = e.touches[0].clientX;
            stopAutoPlay();
            trackContainer.style.opacity = '0.7';
        }, {passive: true});

        container.addEventListener('touchend', (e) => {
            const endX = e.changedTouches[0].clientX;
            const diff = endX - startX;
            trackContainer.style.opacity = '1';
            
            if (Math.abs(diff) > 50) {
                if (diff > 0) {
                    moveToSlide(currentIndex - 1);
                } else {
                    moveToSlide(currentIndex + 1);
                }
            }
            startAutoPlay();
        }, {passive: true});
    }

    // Init
    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    if (urlParams.get('debug_zones') === '1') {
        container.classList.add('debug-zones');
    }

    // Initialize players for any static iframes that might exist
    const initStaticPlayers = () => {
         const staticIframes = track.querySelectorAll('iframe');
         staticIframes.forEach((iframe, index) => {
             if (!iframe.id) iframe.id = `static-brand-video-${index}`;
             // Only init if not already tracked
             if (!ytPlayers[iframe.id]) {
                 pendingPlayers.push({ id: iframe.id, videoId: null }); // videoId null implies auto-detect from src? 
                 // Actually YT.Player needs videoId OR it can take over existing iframe.
                 // If we pass ID of existing iframe, it takes it over.
             }
         });
         if (window.YT) processPendingPlayers();
         else loadYouTubeAPI();
    };

    startAutoPlay();
    initDynamicCarousel();
    initStaticPlayers();
});
</script>

                        <a class="lang-link" role="option" aria-selected="false" data-locale="en-hk" data-code="86" data-url="mainland-china" href="/en-hk/mainland-china/lucky-phone-number/pricebook-mainland-china" aria-label="中國大陸 English">Eng</a>
                      </div>
