            <script>
            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
                // Accordion Functionality
                const headers = document.querySelectorAll('.accordion-header');
                
                headers.forEach(header => {
                    header.addEventListener('click', function() {
                        const content = this.nextElementSibling;
                        const indicator = this.querySelector('.accordion-indicator');
                        const isOpen = content.classList.contains('open');
                        
                        if (isOpen) {
                            content.classList.remove('open');
                            content.style.maxHeight = null;
                            indicator.textContent = '+';
                            this.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
                        } else {
                            content.classList.add('open');
                            content.style.maxHeight = content.scrollHeight + "px";
                            indicator.textContent = '-';
                            this.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
                        }
                    });
                    
                    // Keyboard support for header
                    header.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
                        if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            this.click();
                        }
                    });
                });

                // Search Functionality within Sections
                const searchInputs = document.querySelectorAll('.section-search-input');
                
                searchInputs.forEach(input => {
                    input.addEventListener('input', function() {
                        const searchTerm = this.value.toLowerCase();
                        const section = this.closest('.accordion-content');
                        const items = section.querySelectorAll('.searchable-item');
                        const noResults = section.querySelector('.no-results');
                        let hasVisible = false;

                        items.forEach(item => {
                            const searchData = (item.getAttribute('data-search') || '').toLowerCase();
                            const textContent = item.textContent.toLowerCase();
                            
                            if (searchData.includes(searchTerm) || textContent.includes(searchTerm)) {
                                item.classList.remove('hidden');
                                hasVisible = true;
                            } else {
                                item.classList.add('hidden');
                            }
                        });

                        if (hasVisible) {
                            noResults.style.display = 'none';
                        } else {
                            noResults.style.display = 'block';
                        }
                        
                        // Recalculate height for transition
                        if (section.classList.contains('open')) {
                             section.style.maxHeight = section.scrollHeight + "px";
                        }
                    });
                    
                    // Prevent collapse when clicking search
                    input.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        e.stopPropagation();
                    });
                });

                // ===== STV TreeView (shared JS) =====
                function stvGetNodeLabel(node) {
                    if (!node) return '';
                    var label = (node.tag_zh_hk || '').trim();
                    if (label) return label;
                    return (node.tag_name || '').trim();
                }

                function stvBuildNode(node, level, colKey) {
                    var labelText = stvGetNodeLabel(node);
                    if (!labelText) return null;

                    var li = document.createElement('li');
                    li.id = 'stv_' + colKey + '_node_' + node.id;
                    var searchTokens = [];
                    var zhLabel = (node.tag_zh_hk || '').trim();
                    var enLabel = (node.tag_name || '').trim();
                    if (zhLabel) searchTokens.push(zhLabel);
                    if (enLabel) searchTokens.push(enLabel);
                    if (node.id !== undefined && node.id !== null) {
                        searchTokens.push(String(node.id));
                    }
                    if (searchTokens.length > 0) {
                        li.setAttribute('data-search', searchTokens.join(' '));
                    }

                    var hasChildren = Array.isArray(node.children) && node.children.length > 0;
                    if (hasChildren) {
                        var icon = document.createElement('i');
                        icon.className = 'caret stv_plus';
                        icon.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
                        li.appendChild(icon);
                    }

                    var inputId = hasChildren
                        ? ('stv_' + colKey + '_c_' + node.id)
                        : ((node.tag_name || '').trim() !== '' ? node.tag_name : ('stv_' + colKey + '_leaf_' + node.id));

                    var label = document.createElement('label');
                    label.className = 'stv_label';
                    label.setAttribute('for', inputId);

                    var input = document.createElement('input');
                    input.type = 'checkbox';
                    input.id = inputId;

                    var span = document.createElement('span');
                    span.textContent = labelText;

                    label.appendChild(input);
                    label.appendChild(span);
                    li.appendChild(label);

                    if (hasChildren) {
                        var ul = document.createElement('ul');
                        ul.className = level === 1 ? 'stv_sub_ul' : 'stv_inner_ul';
                        ul.style.display = 'none';
                        node.children.forEach(function(child) {
                            var childLi = stvBuildNode(child, level + 1, colKey);
                            if (childLi) ul.appendChild(childLi);
                        });
                        li.appendChild(ul);
                    }
                    return li;
                }

                function stvRenderMenuFromData(data) {
                    var mount = document.getElementById('advsearch_menu_mount');
                    if (!mount || !data || !Array.isArray(data.columns)) return;
                    mount.innerHTML = '';

                    var container = document.createElement('div');
                    container.className = 'stv_columns-container';

                    data.columns.forEach(function(col, idx) {
                        var colKey = col.key || (idx === 0 ? 'left' : (idx === 1 ? 'right' : ('col' + (idx + 1))));
                        var column = document.createElement('div');
                        column.className = 'stv_column';
                        column.setAttribute('data-stv-name', colKey);

                        var title = document.createElement('div');
                        title.className = 'stv_column-title';
                        title.textContent = col.title || '分類';
                        column.appendChild(title);

                        var tree = document.createElement('div');
                        tree.className = 'stv_tree_main';
                        tree.id = 'stv_' + colKey + '_tree';

                        var ul = document.createElement('ul');
                        ul.className = 'stv_main_ul';
                        ul.id = 'stv_' + colKey + '_main';

                        (col.nodes || []).forEach(function(node) {
                            var li = stvBuildNode(node, 1, colKey);
                            if (li) ul.appendChild(li);
                        });

                        tree.appendChild(ul);
                        column.appendChild(tree);
                        container.appendChild(column);
                    });

                    mount.appendChild(container);
                }

                if (window.AdvSearchMenuData) {
                    stvRenderMenuFromData(window.AdvSearchMenuData);
                }

                function stvInitTreeInColumn(columnEl) {
                    const tree = columnEl.querySelector('.stv_tree_main');
                    if (!tree) return;

                    // Toggle expand/collapse
                    tree.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        const toggle = e.target.closest('.stv_plus, .stv_minus');
                        const label = e.target.closest('label.stv_label');
                        let li = null;

                        // icon click
                        if (toggle && tree.contains(toggle)) {
                            li = toggle.closest('li');
                        }

                        // label click: only for nodes that have children (Level 1/2); ignore Level 3 with visible checkbox
                        if (!li && label && tree.contains(label)) {
                            const maybeLi = label.closest('li');
                            const childUl = maybeLi ? Array.from(maybeLi.children).find(el => el && el.tagName === 'UL') : null;
                            const checkbox = label.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
                            const checkboxVisible = checkbox && checkbox.offsetParent !== null;
                            if (childUl && !checkboxVisible) {
                                // Level 1/2: prevent checkbox toggling; only expand/collapse
                                e.preventDefault();
                                e.stopPropagation();
                                li = maybeLi;
                            }
                        }

                        if (!li) return;
                        const childUl = Array.from(li.children).find(el => el && el.tagName === 'UL');
                        if (!childUl) return;

                        const icon = li.querySelector(':scope > .stv_plus, :scope > .stv_minus');
                        const isHidden = childUl.style.display === 'none';
                        childUl.style.display = isHidden ? '' : 'none';
                        if (icon) {
                            icon.classList.toggle('stv_minus', isHidden);
                            icon.classList.toggle('stv_plus', !isHidden);
                            /* 移除 transform 動畫覆蓋，改用 transition 展示旋轉 */
                        }
                    });

                    // Checkbox cascade (down + up)
                    tree.addEventListener('change', function(e) {
                        const cb = e.target;
                        if (!cb || cb.tagName !== 'INPUT' || cb.type !== 'checkbox') return;
                        const li = cb.closest('li');
                        if (!li) return;

                        // Down
                        li.querySelectorAll('ul input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(child => {
                            child.checked = cb.checked;
                        });

                        // Up
                        let currentLi = li;
                        while (true) {
                            const parentUl = currentLi.parentElement;
                            if (!parentUl || parentUl.tagName !== 'UL') break;
                            const parentLi = parentUl.closest('li');
                            if (!parentLi || !tree.contains(parentLi)) break;

                            const childLis = Array.from(parentUl.children).filter(el => el.tagName === 'LI');
                            const childCbs = childLis
                                .map(x => x.querySelector(':scope > label > input[type="checkbox"]') || x.querySelector(':scope > input[type="checkbox"]'))
                                .filter(Boolean);

                            const allChecked = childCbs.length > 0 && childCbs.every(x => x.checked);
                            const parentCb = parentLi.querySelector(':scope > label > input[type="checkbox"]') || parentLi.querySelector(':scope > input[type="checkbox"]');
                            if (parentCb) parentCb.checked = allChecked;

                            currentLi = parentLi;
                        }
                    });
                }

                document.querySelectorAll('.stv_columns-container .stv_column').forEach(stvInitTreeInColumn);

                // Inject custom checkmark span for Level 3 checkboxes
                function stvInjectLv3Checkmarks() {
                    document.querySelectorAll('.stv_inner_ul label.stv_label').forEach(label => {
                        // Avoid duplicate insertion
                        if (label.querySelector('.stv_l3_checkmark')) return;
                        const textSpan = label.querySelector('span');
                        const checkmark = document.createElement('span');
                        checkmark.className = 'stv_l3_checkmark';
                        if (textSpan) {
                            label.insertBefore(checkmark, textSpan);
                        } else {
                            label.appendChild(checkmark);
                        }
                    });
                }
                stvInjectLv3Checkmarks();

                function stvApplySearch(tree, term) {
                    const lis = Array.from(tree.querySelectorAll('li'));
                    if (!term) {
                        lis.forEach(li => li.classList.remove('stv_hidden'));
                        return;
                    }

                    // Hide all
                    lis.forEach(li => li.classList.add('stv_hidden'));

                    // Show matches + ancestors, expand parents
                    lis.forEach(li => {
                        const ownTextEl = li.querySelector(':scope > label span:not(.stv_l3_checkmark)');
                        const ownText = (ownTextEl ? ownTextEl.textContent : li.textContent || '').toLowerCase();
                        const searchData = (li.getAttribute('data-search') || '').toLowerCase();
                        const combined = (searchData ? (searchData + ' ') : '') + ownText;
                        if (!combined.includes(term)) return;

                        li.classList.remove('stv_hidden');

                        // Reveal ancestors + expand their ULs
                        let p = li.parentElement;
                        while (p && p !== tree) {
                            if (p.tagName === 'UL') {
                                p.style.display = '';
                                const pli = p.closest('li');
                                if (pli && tree.contains(pli)) {
                                    pli.classList.remove('stv_hidden');
                                    const icon = pli.querySelector(':scope > .stv_plus, :scope > .stv_minus');
                                    if (icon) {
                                        icon.classList.add('stv_minus');
                                        icon.classList.remove('stv_plus');
                                    }
                                }
                            } else if (p.tagName === 'LI') {
                                p.classList.remove('stv_hidden');
                            }
                            p = p.parentElement;
                        }
                    });
                }

                const stvSearchInput = document.getElementById('stv_searchInput');
                if (stvSearchInput) {
                    stvSearchInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
                        const term = (this.value || '').toLowerCase().trim();
                        document.querySelectorAll('.stv_columns-container .stv_tree_main').forEach(tree => {
                            stvApplySearch(tree, term);
                        });
                    });
                }
            });
            </script>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        var searchInput = document.getElementById('search_text1');
        var optionsRow = document.getElementById('search-options-row');
        var searchWrapper = searchInput ? searchInput.closest('.search-input-wrapper') : null;
        var areaLengthMap = {"852":8,"86":11,"853":8,"60":10,"65":8,"66":10,"44":11,"61":9};
        var currentAreaCodeValue = "852";
        var defaultPhoneLength = 11;
        function areaCodeFromPath() {
            var path = window.location.pathname || '';
            var segs = path.split('/').filter(Boolean);
            var slug = segs[1] || '';
            switch (slug) {
                case 'hong-kong': return '852';
                case 'mainland-china': return '86';
                case 'macau': return '853';
                case 'malaysia': return '60';
                case 'singapore': return '65';
                case 'thailand': return '66';
                case 'united-kingdom': return '44';
                case 'australia': return '61';
                default: return '';
            }
        }
        function applyPreciseSearchLength() {
            var container = document.querySelector('.precise-search-inputs');
            if (!container) return;
            var code = String(currentAreaCodeValue || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
            if (!code) {
                code = areaCodeFromPath();
            }
            var len = (areaLengthMap && areaLengthMap[code]) ? parseInt(areaLengthMap[code], 10) : 0;
            if (!len || len <= 0) {
                len = defaultPhoneLength;
            }
            container.querySelectorAll('.precise-search-item').forEach(function(item, idx) {
                var input = item.querySelector('input');
                if (idx < len) {
                    item.style.display = '';
                    if (input) { input.disabled = false; }
                } else {
                    item.style.display = 'none';
                    if (input) {
                        input.value = '';
                        input.disabled = true;
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        function hideNavForSearch(done) {
            var nav = document.querySelector('.ic-nav');
            if (!nav) {
                if (typeof done === 'function') done();
                return;
            }
            var alreadyHidden = nav.classList.contains('fade-out') || nav.getAttribute('aria-hidden') === 'true';
            nav.classList.add('fade-out');
            document.body.classList.add('nav-hidden');
            nav.setAttribute('aria-hidden','true');
            if (alreadyHidden) {
                if (typeof done === 'function') done();
                return;
            }
            var called = false;
            function finish() {
                if (called) return;
                called = true;
                if (typeof done === 'function') done();
            }
            nav.addEventListener('transitionend', finish, { once: true });
            setTimeout(finish, 350);
        }
        function scrollSearchIntoView() {
            if (!searchInput) return;
            var wrapper = searchInput.closest('.search-input-wrapper');
            var target = wrapper || searchInput;
            var rect = target.getBoundingClientRect();
            var top = window.scrollY + rect.top - 50;
            if (top < 0) top = 0;
            var start = window.scrollY;
            var distance = top - start;
            var duration = 500; // ms
            var startTime = null;

            function easeInOutQuad(t) {
                return t < 0.5 ? 2 * t * t : 1 - Math.pow(-2 * t + 2, 2) / 2;
            }

            function step(timestamp) {
                if (!startTime) startTime = timestamp;
                var elapsed = timestamp - startTime;
                var progress = Math.min(elapsed / duration, 1);
                var eased = easeInOutQuad(progress);
                window.scrollTo(0, start + distance * eased);
                if (elapsed < duration) {
                    window.requestAnimationFrame(step);
                }
            }

            window.requestAnimationFrame(step);
        }
        
        function showSearchOptions() {
            optionsRow.style.maxHeight = '4000px'; 
            optionsRow.style.opacity = '1';
        }
        
        function hideSearchOptions() {
            optionsRow.style.maxHeight = '0';
            optionsRow.style.opacity = '0';
        }

        applyPreciseSearchLength();
        function measureTextWidth(text, font) {
            var canvas = measureTextWidth.canvas || (measureTextWidth.canvas = document.createElement('canvas'));
            var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
            ctx.font = font;
            return ctx.measureText(text).width;
        }

        function updatePlaceholderSize() {
            if (!searchInput || !searchWrapper) return;
            var text = searchInput.getAttribute('placeholder') || '';
            if (!text) return;
            var computed = window.getComputedStyle(searchInput);
            var font = computed.font || (computed.fontSize + ' ' + computed.fontFamily);
            var paddingLeft = parseFloat(computed.paddingLeft) || 0;
            var paddingRight = parseFloat(computed.paddingRight) || 0;
            var available = Math.max(0, searchInput.clientWidth - paddingLeft - paddingRight);
            var textWidth = measureTextWidth(text, font);
            if (textWidth > available) {
                searchWrapper.classList.add('placeholder-small');
            } else {
                searchWrapper.classList.remove('placeholder-small');
            }
        }
        updatePlaceholderSize();
        window.addEventListener('resize', updatePlaceholderSize);
        
        /*
        function toggleSearchOptions(e) {
            // Prevent event bubbling if needed, though usually fine
            // e.stopPropagation(); 
            
            if (optionsRow.style.maxHeight === '0px' || optionsRow.style.maxHeight === '' || optionsRow.style.maxHeight === '0') {
                showSearchOptions();
            } else {
                hideSearchOptions();
            }
        }
        
        function isSearchOptionsVisible() {
            return optionsRow.style.maxHeight !== '0px' && 
                   optionsRow.style.maxHeight !== '' && 
                   optionsRow.style.maxHeight !== '0' &&
                   optionsRow.style.opacity !== '0';
        }
        */

        if (searchInput) {
            searchInput.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.stopPropagation();
                hideNavForSearch(function() {
                    scrollSearchIntoView();
                });
                // Only open advanced search if it's closed, don't close it when clicking search box
                if (optionsRow.style.maxHeight === '0px' || optionsRow.style.maxHeight === '' || optionsRow.style.maxHeight === '0') {
                    showSearchOptions();
                }
            });

            // Autocomplete / Search Results Logic
            var searchResultsContainer = document.getElementById('search_results_container');
            var selectedMultiSearchTagsInline = document.getElementById('selected_multi_search_tags_inline');
            var searchRequestToken = 0;

            searchInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
                var searchTerm = this.value.trim();
                if (searchTerm.length > 0) {
                    displayDummyResults(searchTerm);
                    searchResultsContainer.style.display = 'block';
                } else {
                    searchResultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
                    searchResultsContainer.innerHTML = '';
                }
            });

            searchInput.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
                if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                    var searchTerm = this.value.trim();
                    if (searchTerm.length > 0) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        submitSearch();
                    }
                }
            });

            async function displayDummyResults(term) {
                searchResultsContainer.innerHTML = ''; // Clear previous results
                var columnsWrapper = document.createElement('div');
                columnsWrapper.classList.add('search-results-columns');
                var apiColumn = document.createElement('div');
                apiColumn.classList.add('search-results-col', 'search-results-col-api');
                var otherColumn = document.createElement('div');
                otherColumn.classList.add('search-results-col', 'search-results-col-other');
                var apiHeader = document.createElement('div');
                apiHeader.classList.add('search-results-header', 'blue');
                var apiHeaderAnimationBefore = document.createElement('span');
                apiHeaderAnimationBefore.classList.add('animation');
                apiHeaderAnimationBefore.style.animationDelay = (-Math.random() * 0.6).toFixed(2) + 's';
                apiHeader.appendChild(apiHeaderAnimationBefore);
                apiHeader.appendChild(document.createTextNode('電話號碼'));
                var apiHeaderAnimationAfter1 = document.createElement('span');
                apiHeaderAnimationAfter1.classList.add('animation');
                apiHeaderAnimationAfter1.style.animationDelay = (-Math.random() * 0.6).toFixed(2) + 's';
                apiHeader.appendChild(apiHeaderAnimationAfter1);
                var apiHeaderAnimationAfter2 = document.createElement('span');
                apiHeaderAnimationAfter2.classList.add('animation');
                apiHeaderAnimationAfter2.style.animationDelay = (-Math.random() * 0.6).toFixed(2) + 's';
                apiHeader.appendChild(apiHeaderAnimationAfter2);
                apiColumn.appendChild(apiHeader);
                var aiHeader = document.createElement('div');
                aiHeader.classList.add('search-results-header', 'green');
                var aiHeaderAnimationBefore = document.createElement('span');
                aiHeaderAnimationBefore.classList.add('animation');
                aiHeaderAnimationBefore.style.animationDelay = (-Math.random() * 0.6).toFixed(2) + 's';
                aiHeader.appendChild(aiHeaderAnimationBefore);
                aiHeader.appendChild(document.createTextNode('AI工具'));
                var aiHeaderAnimationAfter = document.createElement('span');
                aiHeaderAnimationAfter.classList.add('animation');
                aiHeaderAnimationAfter.style.animationDelay = (-Math.random() * 0.6).toFixed(2) + 's';
                aiHeader.appendChild(aiHeaderAnimationAfter);
                var aiSection = document.createElement('div');
                var categoryHeader = document.createElement('div');
                categoryHeader.classList.add('search-results-header', 'black');
                categoryHeader.appendChild(document.createTextNode('分類'));
                var categoryHeaderAnimation = document.createElement('span');
                categoryHeaderAnimation.classList.add('animation');
                categoryHeaderAnimation.style.animationDelay = (-Math.random() * 0.6).toFixed(2) + 's';
                categoryHeader.appendChild(categoryHeaderAnimation);
                var categorySection = document.createElement('div');
                otherColumn.appendChild(aiHeader);
                otherColumn.appendChild(aiSection);
                otherColumn.appendChild(categoryHeader);
                otherColumn.appendChild(categorySection);
                columnsWrapper.appendChild(apiColumn);
                columnsWrapper.appendChild(otherColumn);
                searchResultsContainer.appendChild(columnsWrapper);
                var dummyResults = [];
                var apiLoading = null;
                var requestToken = ++searchRequestToken;
                var numericTerm = String(term || '').replace(/\s+/g, '');
                if (requestToken !== searchRequestToken) {
                    return;
                }
                function renderResults() {
                    if (requestToken !== searchRequestToken) {
                        return;
                    }
                    dummyResults.forEach(function(result) {
                        var resultItem = document.createElement('div');
                        resultItem.classList.add('search-result-item', 'type-' + result.type);
                        if (result.api) {
                            resultItem.classList.add('api-phone');
                        }
                        if (result.copyable) {
                            resultItem.classList.add('has-copy');
                            var textSpan = document.createElement('span');
                            textSpan.classList.add('result-text');
                            textSpan.textContent = result.text;
                            resultItem.appendChild(textSpan);
                            var copyButton = document.createElement('button');
                            copyButton.type = 'button';
                            copyButton.classList.add('copySingleNum');
                            copyButton.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Copy phone number');
                            // var tooltip = document.createElement('span');
                            // tooltip.classList.add('tooltip');
                            // tooltip.setAttribute('data-text-end', '已複製');
                            // tooltip.setAttribute('data-text-initial', '複製');
                            // copyButton.appendChild(tooltip);
                            var iconsWrapper = document.createElement('span');
                            var clipboardIcon = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'svg');
                            clipboardIcon.setAttribute('viewBox', '0 0 6.35 6.35');
                            clipboardIcon.setAttribute('width', '15');
                            clipboardIcon.setAttribute('height', '15');
                            clipboardIcon.classList.add('clipboard');
                            var clipboardUse = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'use');
                            clipboardUse.setAttribute('href', '#icon-clipboard');
                            clipboardIcon.appendChild(clipboardUse);
                            var checkIcon = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'svg');
                            checkIcon.setAttribute('viewBox', '0 0 24 24');
                            checkIcon.setAttribute('width', '13');
                            checkIcon.setAttribute('height', '13');
                            checkIcon.classList.add('checkmark');
                            var checkUse = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'use');
                            checkUse.setAttribute('href', '#icon-checkmark');
                            checkIcon.appendChild(checkUse);
                            iconsWrapper.appendChild(clipboardIcon);
                            iconsWrapper.appendChild(checkIcon);
                            copyButton.appendChild(iconsWrapper);
                            copyButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                e.stopPropagation();
                                var value = result.copyValue || result.text;
                                if (navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.writeText) {
                                    navigator.clipboard.writeText(value);
                                } else {
                                    var tempInput = document.createElement('input');
                                    tempInput.value = value;
                                    document.body.appendChild(tempInput);
                                    tempInput.select();
                                    document.execCommand('copy');
                                    document.body.removeChild(tempInput);
                                }
                                copyButton.focus({ preventScroll: true });
                            });
                            resultItem.appendChild(copyButton);
                        } else {
                            resultItem.textContent = result.text;
                        }
                        resultItem.addEventListener('click', function() {
                            if (result.type === 1) {
                                window.location.href = result.url;
                            } else if (result.type === 2) {
                                addMultiSearchTag(result.value, result.tagId, result.checkboxId);
                                searchInput.value = ''; // Clear input after adding tag
                                searchResultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
                            }
                        });
                        if (result.api) {
                            apiColumn.appendChild(resultItem);
                        } else if (result.type === 1) {
                            aiSection.appendChild(resultItem);
                        } else {
                            categorySection.appendChild(resultItem);
                        }
                    });
                }

                function addTagMatches() {
                    getMatchingTagNames(term, 10).forEach(function(match) {
                        dummyResults.push({
                            type: 2,
                            text: match.name,
                            value: match.name,
                            checkboxId: match.checkboxId,
                            tagId: match.tagId
                        });
                    });
                }

                if (/^\d+$/.test(numericTerm)) {
                    apiLoading = document.createElement('div');
                    apiLoading.classList.add('search-result-item', 'search-results-loading', 'api-phone');
                    var loadingIcon = document.createElement('div');
                    loadingIcon.classList.add('loading');
                    loadingIcon.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Loading');
                    for (var i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
                        loadingIcon.appendChild(document.createElement('span'));
                    }
                    apiLoading.appendChild(loadingIcon);
                    apiColumn.appendChild(apiLoading);
                    function resolveAreaCode() {
                        var phpCode = '852';
                        var fallback = phpCode || '852';
                        if (typeof currentAreaCode === 'function') {
                            try {
                                var ac = currentAreaCode();
                                if (ac) {
                                    return ac;
                                }
                            } catch (e) {
                                // ignore and fallback
                            }
                        }
                        return fallback;
                    }
                    var areacode = resolveAreaCode();
                    var apiUrl = '/api/get-phone-array.php?areacode=' + encodeURIComponent(areacode) +
                        '&searchno=' + encodeURIComponent(numericTerm);
                    try {
                        var response = await fetch(apiUrl, { credentials: 'same-origin' });
                        if (response.ok) {
                            var data = await response.json();
                            if (Array.isArray(data)) {
                                data.forEach(function(record) {
                                    var displaynumber = String(record.displaynumber || '');
                                    var cleanNumber = displaynumber.replace(/\s+/g, '');
                                    if (!cleanNumber) {
                                        return;
                                    }
                                    dummyResults.push({
                                        type: 1,
                                        api: true,
                                        copyable: true,
                                        copyValue: displaynumber,
                                        text: displaynumber,
                                        url: 'pricebook?q=' + encodeURIComponent(cleanNumber)
                                    });
                                });
                            }
                        }
                    } catch (e) {
                        // ignore API failures and fallback to default suggestions
                    } finally {
                        if (apiLoading && apiLoading.parentNode) {
                            apiLoading.parentNode.removeChild(apiLoading);
                        }
                    }
                    dummyResults.push(
                        { type: 1, text: 'AI搜尋類似: ' + term, url: 'aisearch?searchno=' + encodeURIComponent(numericTerm) },
                        { type: 1, text: 'AI分析: ' + term, url: 'analyze-number?number=' + encodeURIComponent(numericTerm) },
                        { type: 1, api: true, text: '列出號碼包含: ' + term, url: 'pricebook?q=' + encodeURIComponent(numericTerm) }
                    );
                    addTagMatches();
                    renderResults();
                    return;
                }

                addTagMatches();
                renderResults();
            }

            function getMatchingTagNames(term, limit) {
                var keyword = (term || '').trim().toLowerCase();
                if (!keyword) {
                    return [];
                }
                var tagItems = getExistingTagNames();
                var matches = [];
                for (var i = 0; i < tagItems.length; i++) {
                    var item = tagItems[i];
                    var name = item.name || '';
                    var tagId = String(item.tagId || '');
                    var checkboxId = String(item.checkboxId || '');
                    var haystack = (name + ' ' + tagId + ' ' + checkboxId).toLowerCase();
                    if (haystack.indexOf(keyword) !== -1) {
                        matches.push(item);
                        if (matches.length >= limit) {
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
                return matches;
            }

            function getExistingTagNames() {
                var names = [];
                var seen = {};
                var checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll(
                    '.hot-category-grid input[type="checkbox"], .stv_tree_main input[type="checkbox"]'
                );
                checkboxes.forEach(function(checkbox) {
                    var li = checkbox.closest('li');
                    if (li && li.querySelector('ul')) {
                        return;
                    }
                    var text = getCheckboxLabelText(checkbox);
                    if (!text) {
                        return;
                    }
                    if (!seen[text]) {
                        seen[text] = true;
                        var checkboxId = checkbox.id || checkbox.getAttribute('id') || '';
                        var tagId = checkbox.getAttribute('data-target-id') || checkboxId;
                        names.push({ name: text, checkboxId: checkboxId, tagId: tagId });
                    }
                });
                return names;
            }

            function addMultiSearchTag(text, tagId, checkboxId) {
                var tag = document.createElement('span'); // Changed to span as per user request
                tag.classList.add('multi-search-tag');
                if (tagId) {
                    tag.setAttribute('data-tag-id', tagId);
                }
                if (checkboxId) {
                    tag.setAttribute('data-checkbox-id', checkboxId);
                }
                tag.textContent = text;

                var cancelButton = document.createElement('span');
                cancelButton.classList.add('cancel-tag');
                cancelButton.textContent = 'X';
                cancelButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    tag.remove();
                    if (checkboxId) {
                        var checkbox = document.getElementById(checkboxId);
                        if (checkbox) {
                            checkbox.checked = false;
                            checkbox.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
                        }
                    }
                    updateSelectedTagsClearAllLink();
                });

                tag.appendChild(cancelButton);
                selectedMultiSearchTagsInline.appendChild(tag);
                updateSelectedTagsClearAllLink();
                // Ensure input remains focused after adding tag
                searchInput.focus();
            }

            function addAdvSearchTag(text, checkboxId) {
                if (!selectedMultiSearchTagsInline || !checkboxId) {
                    return;
                }
                if (selectedMultiSearchTagsInline.querySelector('[data-checkbox-id="' + checkboxId + '"]')) {
                    return;
                }
                var tag = document.createElement('span');
                tag.classList.add('multi-search-tag');
                tag.setAttribute('data-checkbox-id', checkboxId);
                var checkbox = document.getElementById(checkboxId);
                if (checkbox) {
                    var tagId = checkbox.getAttribute('data-target-id') || checkboxId;
                    if (tagId) {
                        tag.setAttribute('data-tag-id', tagId);
                    }
                }
                tag.textContent = text;

                var cancelButton = document.createElement('span');
                cancelButton.classList.add('cancel-tag');
                cancelButton.textContent = 'X';
                cancelButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    tag.remove();
                    var checkbox = document.getElementById(checkboxId);
                    if (checkbox) {
                        checkbox.checked = false;
                        checkbox.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
                    }
                    updateSelectedTagsClearAllLink();
                });

                tag.appendChild(cancelButton);
                selectedMultiSearchTagsInline.appendChild(tag);
                updateSelectedTagsClearAllLink();
            }

            function removeAdvSearchTag(checkboxId) {
                if (!selectedMultiSearchTagsInline || !checkboxId) {
                    return;
                }
                var tag = selectedMultiSearchTagsInline.querySelector('[data-checkbox-id="' + checkboxId + '"]');
                if (tag) {
                    tag.remove();
                }
                updateSelectedTagsClearAllLink();
            }

            function getCheckboxLabelText(checkbox) {
                var label = checkbox.closest('label');
                if (!label) {
                    return checkbox.value || checkbox.id || '';
                }
                var span = label.querySelector('span:not(.stv_l3_checkmark)');
                var text = span ? span.textContent : label.textContent;
                return (text || '').trim();
            }

            function syncHotCheckboxesForTarget(targetId, checked) {
                if (!targetId) return;
                document.querySelectorAll('.hot-category-grid input[type="checkbox"][data-target-id="' + targetId + '"]').forEach(function(hotCb) {
                    hotCb.checked = checked;
                });
            }

            document.querySelectorAll('.adv-search-container .stv_tree_main input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(function(checkbox) {
                checkbox.addEventListener('change', function() {
                    var text = getCheckboxLabelText(this);
                    if (!text) {
                        return;
                    }
                    if (this.checked) {
                        addAdvSearchTag(text, this.id);
                    } else {
                        removeAdvSearchTag(this.id);
                    }
                    syncHotCheckboxesForTarget(this.id, this.checked);
                });

                if (checkbox.checked) {
                    var text = getCheckboxLabelText(checkbox);
                    if (text) {
                        addAdvSearchTag(text, checkbox.id);
                    }
                    syncHotCheckboxesForTarget(checkbox.id, true);
                }
            });

            document.querySelectorAll('.hot-category-grid input[type="checkbox"][data-target-id]').forEach(function(hotCb) {
                hotCb.addEventListener('change', function() {
                    var targetId = this.getAttribute('data-target-id');
                    if (!targetId) return;
                    var targetCb = document.getElementById(targetId);
                    if (!targetCb) return;
                    targetCb.checked = this.checked;
                    targetCb.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
                });
            });

            // Close search results when clicking outside
            document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (searchResultsContainer && searchResultsContainer.style.display === 'block' &&
                    !searchInput.contains(e.target) && !searchResultsContainer.contains(e.target) && !selectedMultiSearchTagsInline.contains(e.target)) {
                    searchResultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });

            function applyQueryFromUrl() {
                var params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
                var qVal = (params.get('q') || '').trim();
                if (!qVal) {
                    return;
                }
                var parts = qVal.split('Z');
                var simple = parts.shift() || '';
                var tagsPart = parts.join('Z');

                var isSimpleValid = /^\d{1,11}$/.test(simple);
                if (!isSimpleValid) {
                    simple = '';
                }
                if (simple) {
                    if (searchInput) {
                        searchInput.value = '';
                    }
                    if (selectedMultiSearchTagsInline) {
                        var simpleTagText = '包含' + simple;
                        var exists = false;
                        selectedMultiSearchTagsInline.querySelectorAll('.multi-search-tag').forEach(function(tag) {
                            var firstNode = tag.childNodes && tag.childNodes.length ? tag.childNodes[0] : null;
                            var tagText = firstNode && firstNode.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE ? firstNode.textContent : tag.textContent;
                            if ((tagText || '').trim() === simpleTagText) {
                                exists = true;
                            }
                        });
                        if (!exists) {
                            addMultiSearchTag(simpleTagText);
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (tagsPart !== '') {
                    var posDigitMap = {};
                    tagsPart.split('Z').forEach(function(tagId) {
                        tagId = (tagId || '').trim();
                        if (!tagId) return;
                        var checkbox = document.getElementById(tagId);
                        if (checkbox) {
                            checkbox.checked = true;
                            checkbox.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
                        }
                        var m = tagId.match(/^pos(\d{1,2})d(\d)$/);
                        if (m) {
                            var pos = parseInt(m[1], 10);
                            var digit = m[2];
                            if (pos >= 1) {
                                if (!posDigitMap[pos]) {
                                    posDigitMap[pos] = new Set();
                                }
                                posDigitMap[pos].add(digit);
                            }
                        }
                    });
                    Object.keys(posDigitMap).forEach(function(posKey) {
                        var pos = parseInt(posKey, 10);
                        if (!pos || pos <= 0) return;
                        var digits = posDigitMap[pos];
                        if (!digits || digits.size !== 1) return;
                        var digit = digits.values().next().value;
                        var input = document.getElementById('precise-search-' + pos);
                        if (input && !input.disabled) {
                            input.value = digit;
                            input.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
                        }
                    });
                }

                if (simple || tagsPart !== '') {
                    hideSearchOptions();
                }
            }

            var preciseSelectionMap = {};
            var labelToCheckboxId = null;

            function buildLabelToCheckboxMap() {
                if (labelToCheckboxId) {
                    return labelToCheckboxId;
                }
                labelToCheckboxId = new Map();
                document.querySelectorAll('.adv-search-container .stv_tree_main label.stv_label').forEach(function(label) {
                    var span = label.querySelector('span:not(.stv_l3_checkmark)');
                    var text = span ? span.textContent : label.textContent;
                    text = (text || '').trim();
                    if (!text || labelToCheckboxId.has(text)) {
                        return;
                    }
                    var input = label.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
                    if (input && input.id) {
                        labelToCheckboxId.set(text, input.id);
                    }
                });
                return labelToCheckboxId;
            }

            function setCheckboxState(checkboxId, checked) {
                var checkbox = document.getElementById(checkboxId);
                if (!checkbox || checkbox.checked === checked) {
                    return;
                }
                checkbox.checked = checked;
                checkbox.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
            }

            function syncPreciseInput(index) {
                var input = document.getElementById('precise-search-' + index);
                if (!input) return;
                var value = (input.value || '').trim();
                var prevId = preciseSelectionMap[index];
                if (prevId && prevId !== value) {
                    setCheckboxState(prevId, false);
                    preciseSelectionMap[index] = null;
                }
                if (!value) {
                    return;
                }
                if (!/^\d$/.test(value)) {
                    return;
                }
                var labelText = '第' + index + '位置' + value + '字';
                var map = buildLabelToCheckboxMap();
                var checkboxId = map.get(labelText);
                if (checkboxId) {
                    setCheckboxState(checkboxId, true);
                    preciseSelectionMap[index] = checkboxId;
                }
            }

            function focusNextPreciseInput(index) {
                var container = document.querySelector('.precise-search-inputs');
                if (!container) return;
                var items = Array.prototype.slice.call(container.querySelectorAll('.precise-search-item input'));
                var current = document.getElementById('precise-search-' + index);
                if (!current) return;
                var currentIdx = items.indexOf(current);
                if (currentIdx === -1) return;
                for (var i = currentIdx + 1; i < items.length; i++) {
                    var next = items[i];
                    if (next && !next.disabled && next.closest('.precise-search-item').style.display !== 'none') {
                        next.focus();
                        next.select && next.select();
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }

            for (let i = 1; i <= 11; i++) {
                var preciseInput = document.getElementById('precise-search-' + i);
                if (preciseInput) {
                    preciseInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
                        syncPreciseInput(i);
                        if ((this.value || '').trim().length > 0) {
                            focusNextPreciseInput(i);
                        }
                    });
                }
            }

            applyQueryFromUrl();
            for (let i = 1; i <= 11; i++) {
                syncPreciseInput(i);
            }
        }

        function collectSimpleSearch() {
            var value = (searchInput && searchInput.value ? searchInput.value.trim() : '');
            if (!value) return '';
            return /^\d{1,11}$/.test(value) ? value : '';
        }


        function collectCandidateTags() {
            var container = document.getElementById('selected_multi_search_tags_inline');
            if (!container) return '';
            var tags = [];
            container.querySelectorAll('.multi-search-tag').forEach(function(tag) {
                var tagId = (tag.getAttribute('data-tag-id') || tag.getAttribute('data-checkbox-id') || '').trim();
                if (tagId) tags.push(tagId);
            });
            var seen = new Set();
            var deduped = [];
            tags.forEach(function(tag) {
                if (!seen.has(tag)) {
                    seen.add(tag);
                    deduped.push(tag);
                }
            });
            return deduped.join('Z');
        }

        function buildQueryValue() {
            var simple = collectSimpleSearch();
            var tags = collectCandidateTags();
    return [simple, tags].join('Z');
        }

        function clearAllTags() {
            if (searchInput) {
                searchInput.value = '';
            }
            if (selectedMultiSearchTagsInline) {
                selectedMultiSearchTagsInline.innerHTML = '';
            }
            document.querySelectorAll('.adv-search-container .stv_tree_main input[type="checkbox"], .hot-category-grid input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(function(cb) {
                if (cb.checked) {
                    cb.checked = false;
                    cb.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
                } else {
                    cb.checked = false;
                }
            });
            document.querySelectorAll('.precise-search-inputs input').forEach(function(input) {
                input.value = '';
                input.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
            });
            if (searchResultsContainer) {
                searchResultsContainer.style.display = 'none';
                searchResultsContainer.innerHTML = '';
            }
            updateSelectedTagsClearAllLink();
        }

        function clearQueryParamAndReload() {
            try {
                var url = new URL(window.location.href);
                if (url.searchParams.has('q')) {
                    url.searchParams.delete('q');
                    url.search = url.searchParams.toString();
                    window.location.replace(url.toString());
                    return;
                }
            } catch (e) {
                // Fallback to reload if URL parsing fails
            }
            window.location.reload();
        }

        function clearSelectedTagsOnly() {
            if (!selectedMultiSearchTagsInline) {
                return;
            }
            var tags = Array.prototype.slice.call(
                selectedMultiSearchTagsInline.querySelectorAll('.multi-search-tag')
            );
            tags.forEach(function(tag) {
                var checkboxId = tag.getAttribute('data-checkbox-id');
                tag.remove();
                if (checkboxId) {
                    var checkbox = document.getElementById(checkboxId);
                    if (checkbox) {
                        checkbox.checked = false;
                        checkbox.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        function updateSelectedTagsClearAllLink() {
            if (!selectedMultiSearchTagsInline) {
                return;
            }
            var existing = selectedMultiSearchTagsInline.querySelector('.selected-tags-clear-all');
            if (existing) {
                existing.remove();
            }
            var tags = selectedMultiSearchTagsInline.querySelectorAll('.multi-search-tag');
            if (tags.length > 0) {
                var clearLink = document.createElement('a');
                clearLink.href = '#';
                clearLink.className = 'selected-tags-clear-all';
                clearLink.textContent = '清除全部分類';
                clearLink.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    clearSelectedTagsOnly();
                    updateSelectedTagsClearAllLink();
                });
                selectedMultiSearchTagsInline.appendChild(clearLink);
            }
        }

        function submitSearch() {
            var form = document.getElementById('asearch');
            if (!form) return;
            var qInput = form.querySelector('input[name="q"]');
            if (!qInput) {
                qInput = document.createElement('input');
                qInput.type = 'hidden';
                qInput.name = 'q';
                qInput.id = 'search_q';
                form.appendChild(qInput);
            }
            qInput.value = buildQueryValue();
            form.submit();
        }

        var submitButtons = [
            document.querySelector('label[for="search_text1"] .btn'),
            document.querySelector('.search-input-wrapper .fas.fa-search'),
            document.getElementById('adv-search-submit-btn'),
            document.getElementById('adv-search-submit-btn2'),
            document.getElementById('adv-search-submit-btn3'),
            document.getElementById('adv-search-submit-btn4'),
            document.getElementById('adv-search-submit-btn5')
        ].filter(Boolean);

        submitButtons.forEach(function(button) {
            button.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                if (window.fbq) {
                    fbq('track', 'Search');
                }
                submitSearch();
            });
        });

        [
            document.getElementById('adv-search-clear-btn2'),
            document.getElementById('adv-search-clear-btn3'),
            document.getElementById('adv-search-clear-btn4'),
            document.getElementById('adv-search-clear-btn5')
        ].filter(Boolean)
            .forEach(function(button) {
                button.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    clearAllTags();
                    clearQueryParamAndReload();
                });
            });
        
        // Close button for advanced search
        var closeBtn = document.getElementById('adv-search-close-btn');
        if (closeBtn) {
            closeBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.stopPropagation();
                hideSearchOptions();
            });
        }
        
        // Info icon toggle for advanced search
        var infoIcon = document.getElementById('adv-search-info-icon');
        var infoDescription = document.getElementById('adv-search-info-description');
        if (infoIcon && infoDescription) {
            infoIcon.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.stopPropagation();
                infoDescription.classList.toggle('show');
            });
        }
        
        // Removed: Close advanced search menu when clicking outside
        // Now the menu only closes when clicking the close button
    });
    </script>

<script>
(function(){
  var nav=document.querySelector('.ic-nav');
  if(!nav) return;
  var lastY=window.scrollY||0,dir=0,downStart=0,faded=false,ticking=false,shrinkApplied=false;
  var SHRINK_MS = 500, FADE_MS = 2000;
  function applySmall(){ nav.classList.add('nav-small'); document.body.classList.add('nav-small'); }
  function applyLarge(){ nav.classList.remove('nav-small'); document.body.classList.remove('nav-small'); }
  function showNav(){ nav.classList.remove('fade-out'); document.body.classList.remove('nav-hidden'); nav.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false'); }
  function hideNav(){ nav.classList.add('fade-out'); document.body.classList.add('nav-hidden'); nav.setAttribute('aria-hidden','true'); }
  function onScroll(){
    var y=window.scrollY||0;
    if(!ticking){
      window.requestAnimationFrame(function(){
        var newDir = y>lastY?1:(y<lastY?-1:dir);
        if(newDir!==dir){
          dir=newDir;
          if(dir===1){ downStart=performance.now(); }
          else {
            showNav(); faded=false; downStart=0;
            if(y===0){ applyLarge(); shrinkApplied=false; } else { if(shrinkApplied){ applySmall(); } }
          }
        }
        if(dir===1){
          var elapsed = performance.now()-downStart;
          if(!shrinkApplied && elapsed>=SHRINK_MS){ applySmall(); shrinkApplied=true; }
          if(!faded && elapsed>=FADE_MS){ hideNav(); faded=true; }
        }
        if(y===0){ showNav(); applyLarge(); shrinkApplied=false; faded=false; }
        lastY=y; ticking=false;
      });
      ticking=true;
    }
  }
  window.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, { passive: true });
  var t=nav.querySelector('.ic-nav-toggle');
  if(t){
    t.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
    t.addEventListener('click',function(){ var open=nav.classList.toggle('open'); t.setAttribute('aria-expanded',open?'true':'false'); });
  }
  var overlay=nav.querySelector('.ic-nav-overlay');
  function closeMenu(){ if(nav.classList.contains('open')){ nav.classList.remove('open'); var tt=nav.querySelector('.ic-nav-toggle'); if(tt){ tt.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false'); } } }
  if(overlay){ overlay.addEventListener('click',function(){ if(window.matchMedia('(max-width:976px)').matches) closeMenu(); }); }
  document.addEventListener('click',function(e){ if(window.matchMedia('(max-width:976px)').matches){ if(nav.classList.contains('open')){ if(!e.target.closest('.ic-nav-menu') && !e.target.closest('.ic-nav-toggle')) closeMenu(); } } },{ passive: true });
  function isM(){return window.matchMedia('(max-width:976px)').matches}
  // Desktop: keep dropdown open when moving from main item into dropdown
  nav.querySelectorAll('.ic-nav-menu li.has-sub').forEach(function(li){
    var link = li.querySelector('a');
    var dd = li.querySelector('.dropdown');
    if(!link || !dd) return;
    var closeTimer = null;
    function adjustDropdown(){
      if(isM()) return;
      dd.classList.remove('align-right');
      dd.classList.remove('flip-left');
      var rect = dd.getBoundingClientRect();
      var vw = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || 0;
      var inSub = !!li.closest('.dropdown');
      if(inSub){ if(rect.right > vw) dd.classList.add('flip-left'); }
      else { if(rect.right > vw) dd.classList.add('align-right'); }
    }
    function openNow(){ clearTimeout(closeTimer); li.classList.add('open'); adjustDropdown(); }
    function closeLater(){ closeTimer = setTimeout(function(){ li.classList.remove('open'); }, 120); }
    li.addEventListener('mouseenter', openNow);
    li.addEventListener('mouseleave', closeLater);
    dd.addEventListener('mouseenter', openNow);
    dd.addEventListener('mouseleave', closeLater);
  });
  nav.querySelectorAll('.ic-nav-menu li.has-sub > a').forEach(function(a){
    a.addEventListener('click',function(e){ if(isM()){ e.preventDefault(); var li=a.parentElement; li.classList.toggle('expanded'); }});
  });
})();
</script>
